class="caas-body"><div class="caas-iframe-wrapper"><div class="caas-iframe default" style="padding-bottom:56%;"><blockquote data-src="https://delivery.vidible.tv/htmlembed/pid=5668ae6ee4b0b5e26955d6a6/56000e19e4b0e4e194b84b31.html?vid=5f7c60c98250812b8c227aeb&amp;m.loadingplaceholder=1&amp;m.timeline_preview_shape=rectangle&amp;m.embeded=cms_video_plugin_us.edit.huffpost.net&amp;m.sitesection=news&amp;m.timeline_preview_border=3&amp;m.fwkeyvalues=sponsorship%3dsponsorship_name&amp;m.fwsitesection=composer&amp;m.sound=muted"><div class="caas-card-loader"></div><noscript><iframe src="https://delivery.vidible.tv/htmlembed/pid=5668ae6ee4b0b5e26955d6a6/56000e19e4b0e4e194b84b31.html?vid=5f7c60c98250812b8c227aeb&amp;m.loadingplaceholder=1&amp;m.timeline_preview_shape=rectangle&amp;m.embeded=cms_video_plugin_us.edit.huffpost.net&amp;m.sitesection=news&amp;m.timeline_preview_border=3&amp;m.fwkeyvalues=sponsorship%3dsponsorship_name&amp;m.fwsitesection=composer&amp;m.sound=muted"></iframe></noscript></blockquote></div></div><p>President <a href="https://www.huffpost.com/news/topic/donald-trump" data-ylk="slk:Donald Trump" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">Donald Trump</a> immediately removed his face mask when he returned to the White House on Monday evening, despite testing positive for the <a href="https://www.huffpost.com/feature/coronavirus" data-ylk="slk:coronavirus" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">coronavirus</a> less than a week ago and amid an ongoing outbreak among staffers in the West Wing.</p><p>The president <a href="https://www.huffpost.com/entry/donald-trump-released-hospital-coronavirus_n_5f79c7a0c5b64cf6a251aa2e" data-ylk="slk:left Walter Reed National Military Medical Center" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">left Walter Reed National Military Medical Center</a> just minutes earlier after a three-day stay in the hospital. He had been admitted on Friday just hours after he revealed that both he and first lady Melania Trump had tested positive for the virus, a cluster that has since spread through his White House staff and congressional halls of power.</p><div class="twitter-tweet-wrapper"><blockquote placeholder data-theme="light" class="twitter-tweet"><div class="caas-card-loader small fixed-height"></div><p>Only days into his diagnosis, the first thing President Trump does when he gets back to the White House is take his mask off. <a href="https://t.co/kyqvHcSbIl" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:pic.twitter.com/kyqvHcSbIl" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">pic.twitter.com/kyqvHcSbIl</a></p><p>\xe2\x80\x94 Kaitlan Collins (@kaitlancollins) <a href="https://twitter.com/kaitlancollins/status/1313257137599111169?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:October 5, 2020" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">October 5, 2020</a></p></blockquote></div><p>\xe2\x80\x9cI learned so much about coronavirus, and one thing that\xe2\x80\x99s for certain: Don\xe2\x80\x99t let it dominate you. Don\xe2\x80\x99t be afraid of it. You\xe2\x80\x99re going to beat it,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump declared in a <a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/status/1313267615083761665" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:video" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">video</a> shortly after his arrival (more than <a href="https://coronavirus.jhu.edu/map.html" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:210,000 people" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">210,000 people</a> have died of COVID-19 in the U.S.). \xe2\x80\x9cI went, I didn\xe2\x80\x99t feel so good, and two days ago, I could\xe2\x80\x99ve left two days ago, I felt great, like better than I have in a long time. Don\xe2\x80\x99t let it dominate, don\xe2\x80\x99t let it take over your lives, don\xe2\x80\x99t let that happen.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>Reporters noted that several photographers filming Trump\xe2\x80\x99s return to the White House appeared to be near the president as he took off his mask.</p><p>Soon after, Trump released a video of his arrival on Twitter, which includes footage of him without a face covering as military members and White House aides look on.</p><div class="twitter-tweet-wrapper"><blockquote placeholder data-theme="light" class="twitter-tweet"><div class="caas-card-loader small fixed-height"></div><p><a href="https://t.co/Sn4yTTg8eB" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:pic.twitter.com/Sn4yTTg8eB" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">pic.twitter.com/Sn4yTTg8eB</a></p><p>\xe2\x80\x94 Donald J. Trump (@realDonaldTrump) <a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump/status/1313267143232942081?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:October 5, 2020" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">October 5, 2020</a></p></blockquote></div><p>The White House did not immediately return HuffPost\xe2\x80\x99s request for comment. It\xe2\x80\x99s unclear if Trump will wear a mask at the White House while he remains infectious (the Centers for Disease Control and Prevention say that period <a href="https://www.cdc.gov/coronavirus/2019-ncov/hcp/duration-isolation.html" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:could last between 10 and 20 days" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">could last between 10 and 20 days</a>, depending on the severity of the individual case).</p><p><a href="https://www.huffpost.com/entry/trump-condition-coronavirus_n_5f77952fc5b64cf6a250382f" data-ylk="slk:Questions remain" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">Questions remain</a> about the severity of the president\xe2\x80\x99s illness. His medical team has said repeatedly that he is doing \xe2\x80\x9cvery well,\xe2\x80\x9d but outside experts have expressed concern amid reports that Trump\xe2\x80\x99s blood oxygen levels fell below 95% at least twice since he contracted the virus.</p><p>Trump moved quickly to minimize his own infection, regularly tweeting that he is \xe2\x80\x9cfeeling really good!\xe2\x80\x9d while releasing campaign-style videos from inside the hospital and driving outside for a photo op.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cDon\xe2\x80\x99t be afraid of Covid. Don\xe2\x80\x99t let it dominate your life,\xe2\x80\x9d the president posted on Monday shortly before departing Walter Reed. \xe2\x80\x9cWe have developed, under the Trump Administration, some really great drugs &amp; knowledge. I feel better than I did 20 years ago!\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>Trump did acknowledge that he wasn\xe2\x80\x99t feeling well, at least temporarily, in the days after his first positive test as he went to the hospital.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cAs your leader, I had to do that. I knew there\xe2\x80\x99s danger to it, but I had to do it,\xe2\x80\x9d he said in the Twitter video.</p><p>He added: \xe2\x80\x9cI stood out front, I led. Nobody that\xe2\x80\x99s a leader would not do what I did. And I know there\xe2\x80\x99s a risk, there\xe2\x80\x99s a danger, but that\xe2\x80\x99s OK. And now I\xe2\x80\x99m better, and maybe I\xe2\x80\x99m immune, I don\xe2\x80\x99t know.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p>The nation\xe2\x80\x99s top medical officials have continued to urge the use of face masks to minimize the spread of COVID-19. Dr. Anthony Fauci, the director of the National Institute of Allergy and Infectious Diseases, said Monday that a White House event last month to celebrate the nomination of Judge Amy Coney Barrett to the Supreme Court <a href="https://www.huffpost.com/entry/fauci-white-house-trump-dangerous-situation-coronavirus-covid-19_n_5f7b943cc5b61229a055c41b" data-ylk="slk:was the type of \xe2\x80\x9cdangerous situation\xe2\x80\x9d" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">was the type of \xe2\x80\x9cdangerous situation\xe2\x80\x9d</a> he\xe2\x80\x99d long warned about. At least nine attendees have since tested positive for the virus.</p><p>Also on Monday, former Vice President Joe Biden, Trump\xe2\x80\x99s Democratic competitor for the White House, called for the president to \xe2\x80\x9clisten to the scientists\xe2\x80\x9d and implement a nationwide mask mandate.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x9cI would ask him to do this: Listen to the scientists,\xe2\x80\x9d Biden said while speaking in Miami. \xe2\x80\x9cSupport masks. Support a mask mandate nationwide. Require masks in every federal building and facility, and in interstate travel. Urge every governor and mayor to do the same. We know it saves lives.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><div class="twitter-tweet-wrapper"><blockquote placeholder data-theme="light" class="twitter-tweet"><div class="caas-card-loader small fixed-height"></div><p>Masks matter. They save lives.</p><p>\xe2\x80\x94 Joe Biden (@JoeBiden) <a href="https://twitter.com/JoeBiden/status/1313269992360681472?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw" rel="nofollow noopener" target="_blank" data-ylk="slk:October 6, 2020" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">October 6, 2020</a></p></blockquote></div><p>Related...</p><p><a href="https://www.huffpost.com/entry/john-cornyn-trump-coronavirus_n_5f7b93bac5b6e5aba0ce8dd3" data-ylk="slk:GOP Sen. John Cornyn Criticizes Trump On COVID-19: \'A Lesson To All Of Us\'" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">GOP Sen. John Cornyn Criticizes Trump On COVID-19: \'A Lesson To All Of Us\'</a></p><p><a \xe2\x80\x98Dangerous Situation\xe2\x80\x99" class="link rapid-noclick-resp">Fauci: Amy Coney Barrett Nomination Event Was A \xe2\x80\x98Dangerous Situation\xe2\x80\x99</a></p><p><a
